---

<p><em>Many, many thanks to Massimo Cicognani for contributing the code in today’s post. Massimo contacted me as he was working through some issues with his implementation and then kindly offered to share it with this blog’s readers.</em></p>  <p>We’ve looked at a few <a href="http://through-the-interface.typepad.com/through_the_interface/overrules/" target="_blank">different types of overrule</a> on this blog, in the past, and even taken a look at <a href="http://through-the-interface.typepad.com/through_the_interface/2009/08/knowing-when-an-autocad-object-is-grip-edited-using-overrules-in-net.html" target="_blank">a grip overrule</a> or two. Massimo’s much more advanced grip overrule works with a very particular type of polyline: those that alternate between straight and arc segments (with the first and last segments being straight). This might sound a touch specific, unless of course you’re working with such polylines on a regular basis to represent pipes, etc.</p>  <p>The code is split into two C# source files. The first contains the implementation of the overrule and the command to toggle it on and off.</p>  <div style="font-family: courier new; background: white; color: black; font-size: 8pt">   <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">using</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> Autodesk.AutoCAD.Runtime;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">using</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">using</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">using</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> Autodesk.AutoCAD.Geometry;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">using</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> Autodesk.AutoCAD.GraphicsInterface;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">using</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> Autodesk.AutoCAD.EditorInput;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">using</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> System.Collections.Generic;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">using</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> System;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">namespace</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> comsPLine</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">{</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Derived class for grip handling</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">public</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">class</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">myGripData</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> : </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">GripData</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Object id of the original entity</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">public</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">ObjectId</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> m_key = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">ObjectId</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.Null;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Progressive grip number</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">public</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">int</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> m_index = 0;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Previous radius at this grip vertex</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">public</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> m_radius = 0.0;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">public</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">override</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">void</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> OnGripStatusChanged(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Status</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> newStatus</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; )</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (newStatus == </span><span style="line-height: 140%; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">public</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">override</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">bool</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> ViewportDraw(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">ObjectId</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> entityId,</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">GripData</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">DrawType</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> type,</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%">? imageGripPoint,</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">int</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> gripSizeInPixels</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; )</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Calculate the size of the glyph in WCS</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> glyphSize =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; worldDraw.Viewport.GetNumPixelsInUnitSquare(</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">this</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.GripPoint);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> glyphHeight = (gripSizeInPixels / glyphSize.Y);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Transform to viewport</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Matrix3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> e2w = worldDraw.Viewport.EyeToWorldTransform;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> pt = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">this</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.GripPoint.TransformBy(e2w);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Draw a glyph</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3dCollection</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> pnts = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3dCollection</span><span style="line-height: 140%">();</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pnts.Add(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; );</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pnts.Add(</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(pt.X, pt.Y - glyphHeight, pt.Z));</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pnts.Add(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; );</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pnts.Add(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; );</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; worldDraw.Geometry.DeviceContextPolygon(pnts);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// of a given document. In other words, non static data in this</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// class is implicitly per-document!</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">static</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">bool</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> overruling = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// gripdata for each selected polyline</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Dictionary</span><span style="line-height: 140%">&lt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Set event handlers on documents to get access to</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// OnImpliedSelectionChanged</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; dm.DocumentCreated +=</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">DocumentCollectionEventHandler</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(dm_DocumentCreated);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; dm.DocumentToBeDestroyed +=</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">DocumentCollectionEventHandler</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(dm_DocumentToBeDestroyed);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Attach handler to currently loaded documents</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;summary&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> Check if the polyline topology is compatible with a</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> sequence of segments with internal rounded edges.</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> Used to activate an alternate grip handling where</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> user can control segment vertexes through apparent</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> intersections.</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/summary&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;p&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/returns&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">public</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">static</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">bool</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> IsPolylineRoundedEdge(</span><span style="line-height: 140%; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">bool</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> result = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">false</span><span style="line-height: 140%">;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (p != </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">null</span><span style="line-height: 140%">)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Quick check if it contains at least one arc and two</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// segments, that means at least 4 points also check</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// for planar entity</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">SegmentType</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> prevType = p.GetSegmentType(0);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// First segment must be a line</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// either segment forms a rect triangle. Align segment</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// coefficient to X axis, so the radius would be aligned</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// to Y axis</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> cxr = rb.cx * r1.cx + rb.cy * r1.cy;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> cyr = -rb.cx * r1.cy + rb.cy * r1.cx;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Get hypotenuse given the radius and sine coefficient</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> ipo = v.radius / cyr;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Get other catete: distance from pOrg and the fillet</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// points on segments</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> l1 = ipo * cxr;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// If allowed, check if fillet point lays outside the</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// smallest segment lenght</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (bAllowRadiusReduction)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> dmin = (d1 &lt; d2) ? d1 : d2;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (l1 &gt; dmin)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Reduce radius to keep fillet inside segment</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; v.radius = dmin * cyr / cxr;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Use new radius for computation</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; ipo = v.radius / cyr;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; l1 = ipo * cxr;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Given the length, get arc start and end points on</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// each segment. Beware of segment switch, if occurred</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (bInversionOccured)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; v.p2 =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pOrg.X + l1 * r1.cx, pOrg.Y + l1 * r1.cy, 0.0</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; );</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; v.p1 =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pOrg.X + l1 * r2.cx, pOrg.Y + l1 * r2.cy, 0.0</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; );</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">else</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; v.p1 =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pOrg.X + l1 * r1.cx, pOrg.Y + l1 * r1.cy, 0.0</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; );</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; v.p2 =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pOrg.X + l1 * r2.cx, pOrg.Y + l1 * r2.cy, 0.0</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; );</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Get arc midpoint on bisetrix</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; v.pc =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pOrg.X + (ipo - v.radius) * rb.cx,</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pOrg.Y + (ipo - v.radius) * rb.cy,</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; 0.0</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; );</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Get arc origin</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; v.pOrg =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pOrg.X + ipo * rb.cx, pOrg.Y + ipo * rb.cy, 0.0</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; );</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Compute bulge using the formula B = 2*H/D, where D is</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// the chord and H the distance of the chord midpoint</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// and the arc midpoint</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> D = v.p1.DistanceTo(v.p2);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> H = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Math</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.Abs(</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.DistFromLine(v.p1, v.p2, v.pc));</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (D &gt; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon) v.bulge = 2 * H / D;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Bulge should be positive for counterclockwise arcs and</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// negative for clockwise. Adjust sign according with</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// segment order switch, if occurred</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (!bInversionOccured) v.bulge = -v.bulge;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">catch</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Exception</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> ex)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; System.Diagnostics.</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Debug</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.WriteLine(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #a31515">&quot;[LinesFillet]&quot;</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> + ex.Message</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; );</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">return</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">false</span><span style="line-height: 140%">;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">return</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">true</span><span style="line-height: 140%">;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;summary&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> Get plausible fillet radius from two converging linesegments</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/summary&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;l1&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">First segment</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;l2&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">Second segment</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;pPlane&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">Working plane</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;pOut&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">Resulting point, if available</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;returns&gt;&lt;/returns&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">public</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">static</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> GetFilletRadius(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">LineSegment3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> l1, </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">LineSegment3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> l2, </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Plane</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> pPlane</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; )</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> result = 0.0;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Get 2d points on working plane</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> p1 = l1.StartPoint.Convert2d(pPlane);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> p2 = l1.EndPoint.Convert2d(pPlane);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> q1 = l2.StartPoint.Convert2d(pPlane);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> q2 = l2.EndPoint.Convert2d(pPlane);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; )</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> l1_end =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// distances should be the same and equals to the fillet</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;
