color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> Try to get intersection point of two segment.</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> The intersection may be real or apparent.</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> The resulting point is </span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/summary&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;p1&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">Start point of first segment</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;p2&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">End point of first segment</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;q1&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">Start point of second segment</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;q2&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">End point of second segment</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;pInt&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">[out] Resulting intersection point</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;returns&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">Result validity state</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/returns&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">public</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">static</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">IntersectLinesState</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> IntersectLines(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> p1, </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> p2, </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// First segment</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> q1, </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> q2, </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Second segment</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">out</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> pInt&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Intersecting point</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; )</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">IntersectLinesState</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> result =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">IntersectLinesState</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.NoIntersection;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pInt = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.Origin;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Get sine/cosine coefficients for the two segments</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csCosDir</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> r1 = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csCosDir</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(p1, p2);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csCosDir</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> r2 = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csCosDir</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(q1, q2);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Check coefficients, if points are coincident,</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// segments are null</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; (r1.cx == 0.0 &amp;&amp; r1.cy == 0.0) ||</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; (r2.cx == 0.0 &amp;&amp; r2.cy == 0.0)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; )</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Coincident points? Invalid segments data</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">return</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">IntersectLinesState</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.InvalidPoints;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Intersection coefficients</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> a1 = r1.cx, a2 = r1.cy;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> b1 = -r2.cx, b2 = -r2.cy;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> c1 = q1.X - p1.X, c2 = q1.Y - p1.Y;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Get denominator, if null, segments have same direction</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> dden = a1 * b2 - a2 * b1;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Math</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.Abs(dden) &gt; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Valid denominator, lines are not parallels or co-linear</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// now, intersection linear parameter may be get either</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// from first or second segment. Do both to check for</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// real or apparent intersection.</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Linear parameter for second segment</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> tt = (c1 * b2 - c2 * b1) / dden;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Linear parameter for first segment</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> vv = (c2 * a1 - c1 * a2) / dden;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Intersection point from first segment parameter</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; pInt = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point2d</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(q1.X + r2.cx * vv, q1.Y + r2.cy * vv);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// To be &#39;real&#39;, intersection point must lay on both</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// segments (parameter from 0 to 1). Otherwise, we set</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// it as &#39;apparent&#39;. Get normalized linear parameter</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// (at this stage denominator are intrinsicly valid,</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// no need to check for DIVBYZERO)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; tt = tt / p1.GetDistanceTo(p2);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; vv = vv / q1.GetDistanceTo(q2);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Check if both coefficients lay within 0 and 1</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; tt &gt; -</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon &amp;&amp; tt &lt; (1 + </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon) &amp;&amp;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; vv &gt; -</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon &amp;&amp; vv &lt; (1 + </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; )</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; result = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">IntersectLinesState</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.RealIntersect;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">else</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; result = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">IntersectLinesState</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.ApparentIntersect;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">else</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Segments are parallel or co-linear (have same direction).</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Check coefficients for a new connecting segment with</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// points taken from both original segment. If coefficients</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// are the same, segments are co-linear, otherwise are</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// parallel</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csCosDir</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> rx;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Avoid coincident points</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (p1.GetDistanceTo(q1) &gt; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; rx = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csCosDir</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(p1, q1);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">else</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; rx = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csCosDir</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(p1, q2);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Math</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.Abs(rx.cx - r1.cx) &lt; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon &amp;&amp;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Math</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.Abs(rx.cy - r1.cy) &lt; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; )</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Same coefficient, segments lay on the same vector.</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Check if there is any overlapping by checking distances</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// from the two ends of a segments and another end.</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Sum of distances must be equal or higher than segment </span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// length, otherwise they are partially overlapping</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> ll = p2.GetDistanceTo(p1);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">bool</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> bOver1 =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; q1.GetDistanceTo(p1) + q1.GetDistanceTo(p2) &gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; ll + </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">bool</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> bOver2 =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; q2.GetDistanceTo(p1) + q2.GetDistanceTo(p2) &gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; ll + </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; result =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; bOver1 &amp;&amp; bOver2 ?</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">IntersectLinesState</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.Colinear :</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">IntersectLinesState</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.OverLapping;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">else</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Parallel segments, no intersection</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; result = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">IntersectLinesState</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.NoIntersection;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">return</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> result;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;summary&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> Given a vector going from L1 to L2, get the projected</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> distance of point P from the vector.</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> If distance is positive, the point is on the right side</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> of the vector, if distance is negative, the point is on</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> the left side of the vector.</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> Function assume all points lay on the same plane</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/summary&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;l1&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">Vector origin</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;l2&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">Vector direction</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;p&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">Point to get distance from</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;returns&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">Projected distance of P from vector L1-&gt;L2</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/returns&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">public</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">static</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> DistFromLine(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> l1, </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> l2, </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Point3d</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> p</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; )</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csCosDir</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> c = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">new</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csCosDir</span><span style="line-height: 140%">(l1, l2);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">return</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (((p.Y - l1.Y) * c.cx) - ((p.X - l1.X) * c.cy));</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;summary&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> Get bisetrix coefficients of two vectors.</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> Vectors are provided as coefficients and the order must</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> be given in counterclockwise order.</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> This is a 2d computation, vectors must lay on the same plane</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/summary&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;r1&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">First vector</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;r2&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">Second vector</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;param name=&quot;rb&quot;&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">[out]Resulting coefficients</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/param&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;returns&gt;</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">True if bisetrix has been found, false if not</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">///</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green"> (parallel vectors?)</span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: gray">&lt;/returns&gt;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">public</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">static</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">bool</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> FindBisect(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">ref</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csCosDir</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> rb</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; )</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">bool</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> result = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">true</span><span style="line-height: 140%">;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Coefficients may be considered as points of a limited</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// space that goes from -1 to 1</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Origin 0,0 is the intersection of the two vectors and</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// origin of the bisetrix</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Quick check for vectors (almost) co-linear</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> diste =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Math</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.Sqrt(</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; (r2.cx - r1.cx) * (r2.cx - r1.cx) +</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; (r2.cy - r1.cy) * (r2.cy - r1.cy)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; );</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (diste &lt; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Vectors have very similar coefficients, use alternate</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// algorithm for a borderline situation</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> dcx = (r2.cx + r1.cx) * 0.5;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> dcy = (r2.cy + r1.cy) * 0.5;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> dd = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Math</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.Sqrt(dcx * dcx + dcy * dcy);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">if</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> (dd &lt; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">csMath</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.dEpsilon)</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Really same coefficients, could be co-linear or</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// parallel but cannot say because we don&#39;t have</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// points on segments, just direction</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; result = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">false</span><span style="line-height: 140%">;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">else</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Denominator valid, use point distance from vector</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// to get position of the first vector</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> distc =</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; r1.cx * (r2.cy - r1.cy) - r1.cy * (r2.cx - r1.cx);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> dSign = (distc &lt; 0) ? -1.0 : 1.0;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; rb.cx = dSign * dcx / dd;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; rb.cy = dSign * dcy / dd;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">else</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; {</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: green">// Vectors normally spaced, use simpler formula</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> dcx = (r2.cx - r1.cx);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> dcy = (r2.cy - r1.cy);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Double</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> dd = </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: #2b91af">Math</span><span style="line-height: 140%">.Sqrt(dcx * dcx + dcy * dcy);</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; rb.cx = dcy / dd;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; rb.cy = -dcx / dd;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px">&#0160;</p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span><span style="line-height: 140%; color: blue">return</span><span style="line-height: 140%"> result;</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">&#0160; }</span></p>    <p style="margin: 0px"><span style="line-height: 140%">}</span></p> </div>  <p>Before we show how the code works, let’s start by drawing the type of polyline the code will control:</p>  <p><a href="http://through-the-interface.typepad.com/.a/6a00d83452464869e2017c32020d4d970b-pi" target="_blank"><img alt="Our basic polyline" border="0" height="315" src="/assets/image_836296.jpg" style="background-image: none; border-right-width: 0px; margin: 20px auto; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block; float: none; border-top-width: 0px; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-left-width: 0px; padding-top: 0px" title="Our basic polyline" width="374" /></a></p>  <p>Here are its standard grips:</p>  <p><a href="http://through-the-interface.typepad.com/.a/6a00d83452464869e2017d3c305647970c-pi" target="_blank"><img alt="With its normal grips" border="0" height="315" src="/assets/image_312902.jpg" style="background-image: none; border-right-width: 0px; margin: 20px auto; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block; float: none; border-top-width: 0px; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-left-width: 0px; padding-top: 0px" title="With its normal grips" width="374" /></a></p>  <p>When we run the GOO command to toggle our overrule on and redisplay the grips, here’s what we see:</p>  <p><a href="http://through-the-interface.typepad.com/.a/6a00d83452464869e2017c32020d7f970b-pi" target="_blank"><img alt="With overruled grips displayed" border="0" height="315" src="/assets/image_296674.jpg" style="background-image: none; border-right-width: 0px; margin: 20px auto; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block; float: none; border-top-width: 0px; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-left-width: 0px; padding-top: 0px" title="With overruled grips displayed" width="374" /></a></p>  <p>And here’s what happens when we manipulate one of the “corners” via its grip:</p>  <p><a href="http://through-the-interface.typepad.com/.a/6a00d83452464869e2017744df890f970d-pi" target="_blank"><img alt="With an overruled grip in action" border="0" height="315" src="/assets/image_759934.jpg" style="background-image: none; border-right-width: 0px; margin: 20px auto; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block; float: none; border-top-width: 0px; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-left-width: 0px; padding-top: 0px" title="With an overruled grip in action" width="374" /></a></p>  <p>You can see how the overrule maintains the coherence of the overall polyline as you move the grip. Very cool stuff.</p>  <p>Thanks again for sharing this, Massimo! :-)</p>
